ER models have to be studied very, very hard to understand them. When drawing the database model in Semanta Modeler you will be able to understand it very quickly. It is primarily aimed at modeling (relational-) databases, though the same concept can be used to build models of data structures of any kind (internal class models, system components or non-IT structures like organization hierarchies).\r\n\r\nTo aid you in development of relational databases, it brings you powerful tools to translate the semantic model to the target database:\r\n\r\n- A powerful SQL database script generator to create your database from scratch or migrate your database between model versions.
